      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-610a0c46dcbb8d282132d3b0"><div class="row sqs-row" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868220149_267"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12" id="yui_3_17_2_1_1711868220149_266"><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-610a0c47e156ae2e2924d7b6"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.116129s;"><strong>Established since 1983, Bedok Methodist Preschool is located within the spacious compound of Bedok Methodist Church. Nestled in a serene neighbourhood off Bedok Road, our preschoolers enjoy a safe, fun, relaxed and stimulating learning environment with well-resourced indoor and outdoor learning areas. We offer 3-hour Playgroup for children aged 18 months – 2 years old and 4-hour &amp; 6-hour pre-nursery, nursery and kindergarten programmes for children aged 2 – 6 years old.</strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.120968s;"><strong>Our strong team of qualified and experienced educators are well-trained to administer holistic STEM-based and tech-enabled curriculum within a safe and conducive learning environment to attain our desired learning outcomes as well as inculcate our core values and nurture positive learning dispositions in our children. </strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.125806s;"><strong>We adopt play-based, inquiry- and project-based learning approaches suited to age appropriateness as our preschoolers transit from pre-nursery to kindergarten levels to stimulate children’s affinity to curiosity, exploration, discovery and creativity. Our north star is enable our children to maximise their potential and to nurture every child to be a person of Good Character, who is an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur.</strong></p>
</div>

  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.179032s;" class="preSlide slideIn"><em>Principal’s Message</em></h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.183871s;"><strong>MRS AUDREY TAY</strong></p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.18871s;">Hi, I am Audrey, the principal of Bedok Methodist Preschool. It is a joy to be working with a team of committed and loving teachers and staff.</p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.193548s;">I believe that children are capable, resilient and when given a chance, their potential is endless. At Bedok Methodist Preschool, we help children realise their potential through exploration, activities that are age appropriate as well as inculcating values that reflect God’s goodness and love for us. We strive to work in partnership with our parents to help the children achieve greater things through God’s grace and time. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade fadeIn" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.198387s;">Come visit us at Bedok Methodist Preschool !</p>

</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--book-day" id="tab--book-day" href="#tabpanel--book-day" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a4907c390aa72db8e0003/1628064007104/Group+22.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Book Day</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--book-day" id="tabpanel--book-day" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628062309576_11124"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.295161s;"><strong>Book Day was started to promote reading, encourage our children to read, and discover the joy of reading. We set aside a day in the year whereby we invite parents to come in and read to our little ones. On the 2nd Book Day, our K2 children will go to other classes to read to their schoolmates.</strong></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--christian-education-library" id="tab--christian-education-library" href="#tabpanel--christian-education-library" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a4911f7dd0e71a124e671/1628064017274/Group+68.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Christian Education Library</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--christian-education-library" id="tabpanel--christian-education-library" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628062309576_13611"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.3s;"><strong>BMP has a library of Christian books that are loan out to every child. We have a group of parent-volunteers who would come in weekly to facilitate the exchange system so that the children will get a different book each week. We encourage parents to read with their child to build parent-child bonding as well as imparting biblical truths while enjoying a book together.</strong></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--learning-journey" id="tab--learning-journey" href="#tabpanel--learning-journey" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a4918a8ae215645b5a1d7/1628064024328/Group+69.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Learning Journey</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--learning-journey" id="tabpanel--learning-journey" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628062309576_15357"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.304839s;"><strong>Learning journeys are planned for the children to extend children’s learning beyond the classrooms. They provide children with rich, meaningful and authentic experiences as they interact with environment.</strong></p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--cookery-lessons" id="tab--cookery-lessons" href="#tabpanel--cookery-lessons" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a491d7244840303583acf/1628064029592/Group+70.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Cookery Lessons</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--cookery-lessons" id="tabpanel--cookery-lessons" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1628062309576_16912"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.309677s;"><strong>At least once a term, the children will be given the opportunity to cook in class! Children learn different cooking methods and get to savour different flavours and textures. We have cooked and baked foods such as vegetable soup, sushi roll, ondeh-ondeh, muffins, moon-cake, cookies and many more mouth-watering dishes. These lessons teach children the relationship between food and science in a fun way. At the same time, we encourage our children to eat healthy and also plant little seeds of awareness on the culture behind some of these food e.g. sushi, mooncake, etc</strong></p>
</div>

  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.314516s;" class="preSlide">Long Service Award Recipients 2022</h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.319355s;">Four long-service award recipients from Bedok Methodist Preschool (BMP) share insights of their journey as early childhood educators. Albeit playing different roles at BMP for the past 5 to 10 years, common traits of the recipients are their dedication, passion and joy in their faithful service in answer to the calling in the early childhood industry. </p><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.324194s;">We thank God for all our wonderful team of educators and support staff at Methodist Preschools whose unwavering commitment have enabled us to stay true to our north star to nurture every child to be a person of Good Character, who is an Explorer, an Innovator and an Entrepreneur! </p>

<!-- Add Section IDs for anchor links -->
<script>
(function () {
  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');
    var windowPath = window.location.pathname;
    // If page is set to homepage then set the anchor to home. i.e. #home-1
    if (windowPath === '/') {
      windowPath = 'home';
    }

    var anchorID = windowPath.replace('/', '');

    sections.forEach((section, i) => {
      section.id = `${anchorID}-${i+1}`;
    })
  })
})()
</script>

<script>
window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

function myFunction() {
  var winScroll = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  var height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
  var scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
  document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = scrolled + "%";
}
